  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);

  chops-button, a.button, .button {

    background: var(--chops-white);

    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

  .medium-heading {

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <h2>Email display settings</h2>

        <p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>

        <p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





This report describes same behavior affecting two different dialogs, but filing together since they're closely related.



<span class="line"><!---->This report describes same behavior affecting two different dialogs, but filing together since they're closely related.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In Android, the Bluetooth and USB chooser dialogs do not show origin if initiator is opaque because they look only at the initiator frame's LastCommittedOrigin() [1]. A subsequent DCHECK [2] in the Bluetooth code further indicates this code does not expect opaque origins. The dialog uses the return value [3] of url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay() which is an empty string for opaque origins, therefore the dialog shows an empty string.



<span class="line"><!---->In Android, the Bluetooth and USB chooser dialogs do not show origin if initiator is opaque because they look only at the initiator frame's LastCommittedOrigin() [1]. A subsequent DCHECK [2] in the Bluetooth code further indicates this code does not expect opaque origins. The dialog uses the return value [3] of url_formatter::FormatOriginForSecurityDisplay() which is an empty string for opaque origins, therefore the dialog shows an empty string.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Empty origin in dialog can be achieved by an opaque iframe, a non-opaque iframe that creates its own sandboxed iframe, or any other way that allows creation of opaque origins.



<span class="line"><!---->Empty origin in dialog can be achieved by an opaque iframe, a non-opaque iframe that creates its own sandboxed iframe, or any other way that allows creation of opaque origins.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This may be mitigated by a fix for 



<span class="line"><!---->This may be mitigated by a fix for <!----></span>





issue 1375132



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1375132" title="Security: Android: Bluetooth and USB chooser dialogs do not use top-level origin with permission delegation"><!---->issue 1375132<!----></a>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





if the top-level page can never be opaque; otherwise, the code must handle opaque origins. I have not tested top-level page with opaque origin behavior in other OSes, so the issue may exist there as well if it's possible to create an opaque top-level page that can use these APIs.



<span class="line"><!---->if the top-level page can never be opaque; otherwise, the code must handle opaque origins. I have not tested top-level page with opaque origin behavior in other OSes, so the issue may exist there as well if it's possible to create an opaque top-level page that can use these APIs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Bluetooth chooser dialog code:



<span class="line"><!---->Bluetooth chooser dialog code:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/permissions/android/bluetooth_chooser_android.cc;l=32;drc=8ba1bad80dc22235693a0dd41fe55c0fd2dbdabd



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/permissions/android/bluetooth_chooser_android.cc;l=32;drc=8ba1bad80dc22235693a0dd41fe55c0fd2dbdabd"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/permissions/android/bluetooth_chooser_android.cc;l=32;drc=8ba1bad80dc22235693a0dd41fe55c0fd2dbdabd<!----></a>

  const url::Origin origin = frame->GetLastCommittedOrigin(); // [1]



<span class="line"><!---->  const url::Origin origin = frame-&gt;GetLastCommittedOrigin(); // [1]<!----></span>

  DCHECK(!origin.opaque());                                   // [2]



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK(!origin.opaque());                                   // [2]<!----></span>

  ScopedJavaLocalRef<jobject> window_android =

      reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>(this)));

USB chooser dialog code:



<span class="line"><!---->USB chooser dialog code:<!----></span>

Note that the navigator.usb API did not seem to work in slightly-older M106 Stable versions, so please ensure you are in latest Stable or Canary to reproduce USB PoC.

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 106.0.5249.126 Stable, 109.0.5361.0 Canary<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Bluetooth:



<span class="line"><!---->Bluetooth:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?bt



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?bt"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?bt<!----></a>



<br>





2. Tap the iframe to open device chooser.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Tap the iframe to open device chooser.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





USB:



<span class="line"><!---->USB:<!----></span>



<br>





Pre-requisite: USB device connected to Android device, such as external microphone or keyboard.



<span class="line"><!---->Pre-requisite: USB device connected to Android device, such as external microphone or keyboard.<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?usb



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?usb"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/chromium/bt-usb.html?usb<!----></a>



<br>





2. Tap the iframe to open device chooser.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Tap the iframe to open device chooser.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For both scenarios:



<span class="line"><!---->For both scenarios:<!----></span>



<br>





Observed: No origin is shown in dialog.



<span class="line"><!---->Observed: No origin is shown in dialog.<!----></span>



<br>





Expected: Either top-level page origin is shown in dialog, dialog is not shown, or other safer behavior.



<span class="line"><!---->Expected: Either top-level page origin is shown in dialog, dialog is not shown, or other safer behavior.<!----></span>

Other permission-requesting APIs such as navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition() seem to automatically deny the permission request. I think this is the correct behavior as the only alternative is to only allow ephemeral permission grants for opaque origins and the permission storage infrastructure is not set up for that.

The tasks that are needed to resolve this bug are (for each API):



<span class="line"><!---->The tasks that are needed to resolve this bug are (for each API):<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Add checks in Blink for SecurityOrigin::IsOpaque() to the permission requesting APIs which throw a helpful error message so developers understand what is going on. Example from Web Locks: 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Add checks in Blink for SecurityOrigin::IsOpaque() to the permission requesting APIs which throw a helpful error message so developers understand what is going on. Example from Web Locks: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/locks/lock_manager.cc;l=270;drc=b93c76d7f427e3e2267063f03a82aff2bdf66ce8



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/locks/lock_manager.cc;l=270;drc=b93c76d7f427e3e2267063f03a82aff2bdf66ce8"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/modules/locks/lock_manager.cc;l=270;drc=b93c76d7f427e3e2267063f03a82aff2bdf66ce8<!----></a>



<br>





2. Add Web Platform Tests for this behavior.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Add Web Platform Tests for this behavior.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Add checks in //content/browser which call mojo::Receiver::ReportBadMessage() if a renderer for an opaque origin tries to call these APIs. The checks added in (1) should prevent this from ever happening unless the renderer is compromised.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Add checks in //content/browser which call mojo::Receiver::ReportBadMessage() if a renderer for an opaque origin tries to call these APIs. The checks added in (1) should prevent this from ever happening unless the renderer is compromised.<!----></span>



<br>





4. Add tests for these checks.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Add tests for these checks.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The Web Locks example shows that some specifications explicitly call out an API being unavailable to opaque origins. I'm not sure we actually want to specify that in this case because as mentioned in 



<span class="line"><!---->The Web Locks example shows that some specifications explicitly call out an API being unavailable to opaque origins. I'm not sure we actually want to specify that in this case because as mentioned in <!----></span>





comment #7



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c7"><!---->comment #7<!----></a>





 there is a way to handle permission-requesting APIs for opaque origins but it just isn't supported by Chrome's permissions architecture.



<span class="line"><!----> there is a way to handle permission-requesting APIs for opaque origins but it just isn't supported by Chrome's permissions architecture.<!----></span>

Another way to create an opaque top-level page is to open a new page (popup/tab) from a sandboxed frame, although this requires an additional user interaction compared to the CSP: sandbox HTTP header method. The new page will inherit the opener's sandbox flags.



<span class="line"><!---->Another way to create an opaque top-level page is to open a new page (popup/tab) from a sandboxed frame, although this requires an additional user interaction compared to the CSP: sandbox HTTP header method. The new page will inherit the opener's sandbox flags.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





PoC of this method, tested on Windows and Android:



<span class="line"><!---->PoC of this method, tested on Windows and Android:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/open-opaque-page.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/open-opaque-page.html"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/open-opaque-page.html<!----></a>



<br>





2. Interact with sandboxed iframe (click or press any key) to open new page (tab in this case, can also be a popup)



<span class="line"><!---->2. Interact with sandboxed iframe (click or press any key) to open new page (tab in this case, can also be a popup)<!----></span>



<br>





3. Click anywhere on the opened sandboxed page (which is same PoC from report: 



<span class="line"><!---->3. Click anywhere on the opened sandboxed page (which is same PoC from report: <!----></span>





https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/bt-usb-frame.html?usb



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/bt-usb-frame.html?usb"><!---->https://alesandroortiz.com/security/chromium/bt-usb-frame.html?usb<!----></a>





 )



<span class="line"><!----> )<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Observed: No origin is shown in dialog due to opaque origin. `window.origin` of page is `null`.



<span class="line"><!---->Observed: No origin is shown in dialog due to opaque origin. `window.origin` of page is `null`.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Would appreciate it if someone updates the bug title to remove "Android" and maybe change "Bluetooth and USB chooser dialogs" to "Device chooser dialogs" (since it also affects Serial + HID).



<span class="line"><!---->Would appreciate it if someone updates the bug title to remove "Android" and maybe change "Bluetooth and USB chooser dialogs" to "Device chooser dialogs" (since it also affects Serial + HID).<!----></span>

Date: Thu Jan 05 00:39:26 2023



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Thu Jan 05 00:39:26 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Reject Web Bluetooth requests with an opaque origin



<span class="line"><!---->Reject Web Bluetooth requests with an opaque origin<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The Web Bluetooth API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.



<span class="line"><!---->The Web Bluetooth API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Access to the Web Bluetooth API from such contexts should therefore be blocked.



<span class="line"><!---->Access to the Web Bluetooth API from such contexts should therefore be blocked.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Bug: 1375133



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1375133" title="Security: Device chooser dialogs do not show origin if initiator origin is opaque"><!---->Bug: 1375133<!----></a>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Jan 25 22:32:26 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Reject Web HID requests with an opaque origin



<span class="line"><!---->Reject Web HID requests with an opaque origin<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The Web HID API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.



<span class="line"><!---->The Web HID API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Access to the Web HID API from such contexts should therefore be blocked.



<span class="line"><!---->Access to the Web HID API from such contexts should therefore be blocked.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1375133" title="Security: Device chooser dialogs do not show origin if initiator origin is opaque"><!---->Bug: 1375133<!----></a>

Hi Reilly,



<span class="line"><!---->Hi Reilly,<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I tried to figure out how the opaque origin in WebUSB/WebHID service worker case. i.e whether we should have opaque origin check in [1] (WebUSB service worker create()) and [2] (WebHID service worker create()).



<span class="line"><!---->I tried to figure out how the opaque origin in WebUSB/WebHID service worker case. i.e whether we should have opaque origin check in [1] (WebUSB service worker create()) and [2] (WebHID service worker create()).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





By looking at Service Workers spec about opaque origin in [3] and [4], it seems as long as the service worker's worker/window client is an opaque origin, service worker is not available to the clients. And for the extension service worker case, it would always be extension origin. 



<span class="line"><!---->By looking at Service Workers spec about opaque origin in [3] and [4], it seems as long as the service worker's worker/window client is an opaque origin, service worker is not available to the clients. And for the extension service worker case, it would always be extension origin. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





So, do you think it is fair to say we can ignore handling opaque origin for service worker cases?



<span class="line"><!---->So, do you think it is fair to say we can ignore handling opaque origin for service worker cases?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/usb/web_usb_service_impl.cc;l=186;drc=adac219925ef5d9c9a954d189c2e4b8852a4bbed"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/usb/web_usb_service_impl.cc;l=186;drc=adac219925ef5d9c9a954d189c2e4b8852a4bbed<!----></a>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/hid/hid_service.cc;l=200;drc=adac219925ef5d9c9a954d189c2e4b8852a4bbed"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/hid/hid_service.cc;l=200;drc=adac219925ef5d9c9a954d189c2e4b8852a4bbed<!----></a>

<br>





Reject Web Serial requests with an opaque origin



<span class="line"><!---->Reject Web Serial requests with an opaque origin<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The Web Serial API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level



<span class="line"><!---->The Web Serial API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level<!----></span>



<br>





document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then



<span class="line"><!---->document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then<!----></span>



<br>





there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in



<span class="line"><!---->there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in<!----></span>



<br>





permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.



<span class="line"><!---->permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Access to the Web Serial API from such contexts should therefore be



<span class="line"><!---->Access to the Web Serial API from such contexts should therefore be<!----></span>



<br>





blocked.



<span class="line"><!---->blocked.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Date: Wed Mar 08 00:20:01 2023



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Mar 08 00:20:01 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Reject HidService interface requests from opaque origins



<span class="line"><!---->Reject HidService interface requests from opaque origins<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The Web HID API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If a document has an opaque origin then the requests to access Web HID get rejected on renderer side.



<span class="line"><!---->The Web HID API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level document in the frame tree. If a document has an opaque origin then the requests to access Web HID get rejected on renderer side.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To add a second layer of security in case of the renderer process being compromised, responding to the Web HID mojoms from such renderer process should be avoided.



<span class="line"><!---->To add a second layer of security in case of the renderer process being compromised, responding to the Web HID mojoms from such renderer process should be avoided.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>

The Web USB API tracks permissions using the origin of the top-level

<br>





document in the frame tree. If this document has an opaque origin then

<br>





there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in



<span class="line"><!---->there is no way to format the origin for display to the user in<!----></span>



<br>





permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.



<span class="line"><!---->permission prompts or to write their decision in the preferences file.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Access to the Web USB API from such contexts should therefore be



<span class="line"><!---->Access to the Web USB API from such contexts should therefore be<!----></span>

blocked.

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

VRP Panel: Thanks for the reward!



<span class="line"><!---->VRP Panel: Thanks for the reward!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





sinafirooz@ and chengweih@: Thanks for thoroughly fixing the issues! I'm still reviewing the CLs, but PoCs all are verified as fixed on latest Canary on Windows and Android. Some fixes aren't on M112 Stable, but seem like they will be in M113 which will be released as Stable in a few days.



<span class="line"><!---->sinafirooz@ and chengweih@: Thanks for thoroughly fixing the issues! I'm still reviewing the CLs, but PoCs all are verified as fixed on latest Canary on Windows and Android. Some fixes aren't on M112 Stable, but seem like they will be in M113 which will be released as Stable in a few days.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Specifically, the PoC [1] from 



<span class="line"><!---->Specifically, the PoC [1] from <!----></span>





#c12



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c12"><!---->#c12<!----></a>





 still repros on Windows (112.0.5615.49 Stable) and Android (112.0.5615.135 Stable). Does not repro on Windows Canary 114.0.5728.0.



<span class="line"><!----> still repros on Windows (112.0.5615.49 Stable) and Android (112.0.5615.135 Stable). Does not repro on Windows Canary 114.0.5728.0.<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
